                <div class="m-headlineTease__info">
                 <h5 class="o-storyTease__headline m-headlineTease__headline" itemprop="headline">
                  <a class="o-storyTease__link m-headlineTease__link" href="https://www.militarytimes.com/news/your-military/2021/03/21/iran-threatens-uss-cole-style-attacks-on-fort-mcnair-and-a-top-general-sources-say/">
                   Iran threatens ‘USS Cole-style attacks’ on Fort McNair and a top general, sources say
                  </a>
                 </h5>
                 <p class="m-headlineTease__subhead a-body2" itemprop="description">
                  Communications intercepted by the National Security Agency in January showed that Iran’s Revolutionary Guard discussed mounting “USS Cole-style attacks” against the base in the nation's capital, two U.S. intelligence officials told the AP.
                 </p>
                 <div class="m-headlineTease__meta a-subtitle2">
                  <div class="m-headlineTease__author byline" itemprop="author">
                   James LaPorta, The Associated Press
                  </div>
                  <time ata-pb-field-type="text" class="m-headlineTease__publishDate" data-pb-field="formattedDate" datetime="" itemprop="publishDate">

                  </time>

            </h5>
            <figure class="o-storyTease__featuredImage m-headlineTease__image m-lazyWrapper --rendered lazy-wrapper promo-img-container" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
             <img alt="" class="image-lazy" data-original="https://www.armytimes.com/resizer/UhWwUPfHA1J7iFqAoVJ4YW7d0_E=/500x376/filters:quality(100)/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/mco/7WTBAYKPTNFT3FSFYB5QUT6VKA.jpg" src="data:image/jpg;base64,/9j/4AAQSkZJRgABAQAAAQABAAD/2wBDAAQDAwQDAwQEAwQFBAQFBgoHBgYGBg0JCggKDw0QEA8NDw4RExgUERIXEg4PFRwVFxkZGxsbEBQdHx0aHxgaGxr/2wBDAQQFBQYFBgwHBwwaEQ8RGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhoaGhr/wgARCAAOABIDASIAAhEBAxEB/8QAFwAAAwEAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAYHCP/EABYBAQEBAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAACA//aAAwDAQACEAMQAAABdKJmZpvawiCH/8QAHBAAAQQDAQAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAQIDBAUAERMW/9oACAEBAAEFAqacS90GuychWACvQuRnxZIWP//EABgRAQADAQAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAEAAhIh/9oACAEDAQE/AVL9Zms//8QAGhEAAQUBAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAECAxETMv/aAAgBAgEBPwFY65M3H//EACAQAAEEAgEFAAAAAAAAAAAAAAEAAhESAyEQIjEyQVH/2gAIAQEABj8Ca1znRXx9DjupNo+LHh63YgATvZVqvE7X/8QAHBABAAIDAAMAAAAAAAAAAAAAAQARIUFhUZHB/9oACAEBAAE/Iau/Ub2+wuOp0e5UhjLbUfEB2tgwCOFmJ//aAAwDAQACAAMAAAAQvA//xAAXEQEAAwAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAATFh/9oACAEDAQE/EJihq//EABkRAAMAAwAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAABESHR8P/aAAgBAgEBPxBKxqd42f/EABoQAQEAAwEBAAAAAAAAAAAAAAERACExQWH/2gAIAQEAAT8QG75RG6E0rFvETEB2C0xu0n0wx4ISEtiI2mh1mnprytBazyyCrzD3KBSHc79z/9k="/>
             <noscript>
              <img alt="" class="image-lazy" src="https://www.armytimes.com/resizer/UhWwUPfHA1J7iFqAoVJ4YW7d0_E=/500x376/filters:quality(100)/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/mco/7WTBAYKPTNFT3FSFYB5QUT6VKA.jpg"/>
             </noscript>
            </figure>
            <div class="m-headlineTease__info">
             <p class="m-headlineTease__subhead a-body2" itemprop="description">
              Almost everyone sets new resolutions on January 1, but that’s the easy part. Your resolutions might be job related, like scoring higher on your PT test. Or maybe it’s financial, like staying within budget and paying down debt. When it comes to debt, have no fear – there are great financial offers and tools available to help pay off credit card debt and get you back on track.
             </p>
             <div class="m-headlineTease__meta a-subtitle2">
              <div class="m-headlineTease__author byline" itemprop="author">
              </div>
              <time ata-pb-field-type="text" class="m-headlineTease__publishDate" data-pb-field="formattedDate" datetime="" itemprop="publishDate">
               December 17, 2019
              </time>
             </div>
